\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class RCU, class \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}
Split-\/ordered list set (template specialization for \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_desc}{RCU}) 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu}%
 \doxylink{struct_hash}{Hash} table implementation based on split-\/ordered list algorithm discovered by Ori Shalev and Nir Shavit, see
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2003\mbox{]} Ori Shalev, Nir Shavit "{}\+Split-\/\+Ordered Lists -\/ Lock-\/free Resizable Hash Tables"{}
\item \mbox{[}2008\mbox{]} Nir Shavit "{}\+The Art of Multiprocessor Programming"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

See {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_split_list_set}{intrusive\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}} for a brief description of the split-\/list algorithm.

Template parameters\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type of the value to be stored in the split-\/list.
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ type traits, default is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1split__list_1_1traits}{split\+\_\+list\+::traits}}. Instead of declaring {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1split__list_1_1traits}{split\+\_\+list\+::traits}} -\/based struct you can apply option-\/based notation with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1split__list_1_1make__traits}{split\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\bfseries{Iterators}}

The class supports a forward iterator (\doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f2c87cc75df17ac89786d9b7fc6c432}{iterator} and \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a9f9af7fdce306b796a7e3cd49cdea120}{const\+\_\+iterator}). The iteration is unordered.

You may iterate over split-\/list set items only under RCU lock. Only in this case the iterator is thread-\/safe since while RCU is locked any set\textquotesingle{}s item cannot be reclaimed.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
The iterator object cannot be passed between threads

Due to concurrent nature of skip-\/list set it is not guarantee that you can iterate all elements in the set\+: any concurrent deletion can exclude the element pointed by the iterator from the set, and your iteration can be terminated before end of the set. Therefore, such iteration is more suitable for debugging purposes
\end{DoxyWarning}
The iterator class supports the following minimalistic interface\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

 Note, the iterator object returned by {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a730086ffb1a533f013ca86bd43d1d719}{end()}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a87d1183b1ddccf33c0cf0e2b276bd87e}{cend()}} member functions points to {\ttfamily nullptr} and should not be dereferenced.

\begin{DoxyParagraph}{Usage}

\end{DoxyParagraph}
You should decide what garbage collector you want, and what ordered list you want to use. Split-\/ordered list is an original data structure based on an ordered list. Suppose, you want construct split-\/list set based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1general__buffered}{cds\+::urcu\+::general\+\_\+buffered$<$$>$}} GC and {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_lazy_list}{Lazy\+List}} as ordered list implementation. So, you beginning your program with following include\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{general__buffered_8h}{cds/urcu/general\_buffered.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{container_2lazy__list__rcu_8h}{cds/container/lazy\_list\_rcu.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{split__list__set__rcu_8h}{cds/container/split\_list\_set\_rcu.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{namespace\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cc}}\ =\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds::container}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ data\ belonged\ to\ split-\/ordered\ list}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{sturuct}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{foo}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{nKey}};\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ key\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{std::string}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{strValue}}\ \ \ \ ;\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ value\ field}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 The inclusion order is important\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item first, include one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU implementation} ({\ttfamily \doxylink{general__buffered_8h}{cds/urcu/general\+\_\+buffered.\+h}} in our case)
\item second, include file for ordered-\/list implementation (for this example, {\ttfamily \doxylink{container_2lazy__list__rcu_8h}{cds/container/lazy\+\_\+list\+\_\+rcu.\+h}}),
\item then, the header for RCU-\/based split-\/list set {\ttfamily \doxylink{split__list__set__rcu_8h}{cds/container/split\+\_\+list\+\_\+set\+\_\+rcu.\+h}}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Now, you should declare traits for split-\/list set. The main parts of traits are a hash functor for the set and a comparing functor for ordered list. Note that we define several function in {\ttfamily foo\+\_\+hash} and {\ttfamily foo\+\_\+less} functors for different argument types since we want call our {\ttfamily Split\+List\+Set} object by the key of type {\ttfamily int} and by the value of type {\ttfamily foo}.

The second attention\+: instead of using {\ttfamily Lazy\+List} in {\ttfamily Split\+List\+Set} traits we use {\ttfamily cds\+::contaner\+::lazy\+\_\+list\+\_\+tag} tag for the lazy list. The split-\/list requires significant support from underlying ordered list class and it is not good idea to dive you into deep implementation details of split-\/list and ordered list interrelations. The tag paradigm simplifies split-\/list interface.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ foo\ hash\ functor}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Now you are ready to declare our set class based on {\ttfamily Split\+List\+Set}\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cc::SplitListSet<\ cds::urcu::gc<cds::urcu::general\_buffered<>}}\ >,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{foo}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{foo\_set\_traits}}\ >\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{foo\_set}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


You may use the modern option-\/based declaration instead of classic type-\/traits-\/based one\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ,\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cc::opt::hash<\ foo\_hash\ >}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ hash\ functor}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cc::opt::less<\ foo\_less\ >}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ less-\/based\ compare\ functor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{::type}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ >}

\DoxyCodeLine{>\ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{foo\_set}};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 In case of option-\/based declaration using {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1split__list_1_1make__traits}{split\+\_\+list\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction the struct {\ttfamily foo\+\_\+set\+\_\+traits} is not required.

Now, the set of type {\ttfamily foo\+\_\+set} is ready to use in your program.

Note that in this example we show only mandatory {\ttfamily traits} parts, optional ones is the default and they are inherited from {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1container_1_1split__list_1_1traits}{container\+::split\+\_\+list\+::traits}}. There are many other options for deep tuning of the split-\/list and ordered-\/list containers.

Forward iterator 

The forward iterator for a split-\/list has the following features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it depends on underlying ordered list iterator
\item The iterator object cannot be moved across thread boundary because it contains GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that is thread-\/private GC data.
\item Iterator ensures thread-\/safety even if you delete the item that iterator points to. However, in case of concurrent deleting operations it is no guarantee that you iterate all item in the split-\/list. Moreover, a crash is possible when you try to iterate the next element that has been deleted by concurrent thread.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
Use this iterator on the concurrent container for debugging purpose only.
\end{DoxyWarning}

Forward iterator 

The forward iterator for Michael\textquotesingle{}s set is based on {\ttfamily Ordered\+List} forward iterator and has some features\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item it has no post-\/increment operator
\item it iterates items in unordered fashion
\end{DoxyItemize}

You may safely use iterators in multi-\/threaded environment only under RCU lock. Otherwise, a crash is possible if another thread deletes the element the iterator points to.

The iterator interface\+:

Initializes split-\/ordered list of default capacity 

The default capacity is defined in bucket table constructor. See {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1split__list_1_1expandable__bucket__table}{intrusive\+::split\+\_\+list\+::expandable\+\_\+bucket\+\_\+table}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1split__list_1_1static__bucket__table}{intrusive\+::split\+\_\+list\+::static\+\_\+bucket\+\_\+table}} which selects by {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1container_1_1split__list_a75ca90ee62b45c2a87544d534b02fd5d}{container\+::split\+\_\+list\+::dynamic\+\_\+bucket\+\_\+table}} option. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a2ae45b7ca0c41055ef152d51c0de0519}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!SplitListSet@{SplitListSet}}

Initializes split-\/ordered list of default capacity 

The default capacity is defined in bucket table constructor. \doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{contains()}{contains()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_aa77525470b724f8833e96608c0309caa} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns {\ttfamily true} if it is found, and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}}. Otherwise, you may use {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae929db1391b45c46e073e6caa2f8a4bd}{contains( Q const\&, Less pred )}} functions with explicit predicate for key comparing. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ada63998413c24d1b18a6b8c79ee6ebc1}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}}. Checks whether the map contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is similar to {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the map. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae929db1391b45c46e073e6caa2f8a4bd}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!contains@{contains}}

Checks if the set is empty 

Emptiness is checked by item counting\+: if item count is zero then assume that the set is empty. Thus, the correct item counting feature is an important part of split-\/list set implementation. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a932ef09bac6c32bef0f5888e9a67d2cd}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!empty@{empty}}

 Template parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} defines the key type searching in the list. The set item comparator should be able to compare the values of type {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}} and the type {\ttfamily Q}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Deletes {\ttfamily key} from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_erase_func}%
 The function searches an item with key {\ttfamily key}, calls {\ttfamily f} functor and deletes the item. If {\ttfamily key} is not found, the functor is not called.

The functor {\ttfamily Func} interface\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{extractor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{operator()}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{value\_type}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{val}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


Since the key of split-\/list {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}} is not explicitly specified, template parameter {\ttfamily Q} defines the key type searching in the list. The list item comparator should be able to compare the values of the type {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}} and the type {\ttfamily Q}.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a045a283c69ae27b14342394b5bebdbe2} 
std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Iterator, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f2c87cc75df17ac89786d9b7fc6c432}{iterator}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}} \&\&is\+\_\+iterable\+\_\+list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a74b33e3abb85421185d307ebbbdd1c78}{ordered\+\_\+list}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+at (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Iterator const \&}]{iter}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item pointed by iterator {\ttfamily iter} (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} based set) 

Returns {\ttfamily true} if the operation is successful, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. The function can return {\ttfamily false} if the node the iterator points to has already been deleted by other thread.

The function does not invalidate the iterator, it remains valid and can be used for further traversing.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
{\ttfamily erase\+\_\+at}() is supported only for {\ttfamily Split\+List\+Set} based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}}. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_erase_val}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ac0813e79767faec8708232805e1e63e8}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_erase_func}{erase(Q const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ad8e77899f2784acde39124d511b47c53}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Deletes the item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu_erase_func}{erase(Q const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. 函数调用图\+:

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab7636eacfce8c2960b7775a342938292} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts the item with specified {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_hp_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_hp_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key}, unlinks it from the set, and returns it as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that may be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The extracted item is freed automatically when returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object will be destroyed or released. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Extracts an item from the set 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the set, unlinks it from the set, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the item found. If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aff0fafed34cc602948088754cc91c9d2}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

\doxylink{struct_depends}{Depends} on {\ttfamily bucket\+\_\+type} you should or should not lock RCU before calling of this function\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item for the set based on \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu}{Michael\+List} RCU should not be locked
\item for the set based on \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu}{Lazy\+List} RCU should be locked See ordered list implementation for details.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Extracts the item using compare functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_hp_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5e14835406eb6b8a008a6ddc75d08a0d}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aff0fafed34cc602948088754cc91c9d2}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ada5a6c6c638569b385ff29083a6e82a4}{extract(\+Q const\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a94c28f30ed605a0e3b7abd7cd7d836f7}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a94c28f30ed605a0e3b7abd7cd7d836f7} 
std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}} \&\&is\+\_\+iterable\+\_\+list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a74b33e3abb85421185d307ebbbdd1c78}{ordered\+\_\+list}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f2c87cc75df17ac89786d9b7fc6c432}{iterator}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} and returns iterator pointed to the item found (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} -\/based set) 

If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a730086ffb1a533f013ca86bd43d1d719}{end()}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function is supported only for the set based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} 
\end{DoxyNote}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_find_func}%
 The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor may change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the set\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The {\ttfamily key} argument is non-\/const since it can be used as {\ttfamily f} functor destination i.\+e., the functor may modify both arguments.

Note the hash functor specified for class {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5c5dc83748a948c863c9e960e7ccf520}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}
\index{find@{find}!cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}

 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}} \&\&is\+\_\+iterable\+\_\+list$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a74b33e3abb85421185d307ebbbdd1c78}{ordered\+\_\+list}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_abe8e049f756b5ba547bda825af81b645}{\+::value}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f2c87cc75df17ac89786d9b7fc6c432}{iterator}} $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ae8396ff85d63082521e3324820df1009}{\+::type}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate and returns iterator pointed to the item found (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} -\/based set) 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a94c28f30ed605a0e3b7abd7cd7d836f7}{find(\+Q\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set.

If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a730086ffb1a533f013ca86bd43d1d719}{end()}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
This function is supported only for the set based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} 
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_hp_get}%

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the item found as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}. If {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses one GC\textquotesingle{}s guard which can be limited resource.
\end{DoxyNote}

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the pointer to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

Note the compare functor should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU should be locked before call of this function. Returned item is valid only while RCU is locked\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a9f4ce221e181457872bd54e63728ab95} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ab1a910658827d385bc3ee5564bfa1c05}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_hp_get}{get( Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a2df123766832f05e9a7a07cda98379d3}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}
\index{get\_with@{get\_with}!cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_with()}{get\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a2df123766832f05e9a7a07cda98379d3} 
template$<$class RCU, class \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a2a25139622eb9862eb9c03204c1464e5}{raw\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_nonintrusive_SplitListSet_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ac5a8790c2df3bd4a2eb31890c87ff036}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [1/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_ac5a8790c2df3bd4a2eb31890c87ff036} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&\&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function creates a node with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts the node created into the set.

The type {\ttfamily Q} should contain as minimum the complete key for the node. The object of \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily Q}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily Q} is equal to \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a467a3977bba0540cfc5c045d53b7c87a}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}
\index{insert@{insert}!cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{insert()}{insert()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/4]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a467a3977bba0540cfc5c045d53b7c87a} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&\&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted.

The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp}{Michael\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the set
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this set\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

The function applies RCU lock internally. 函数调用图\+:

Inserts new node 

The function creates a node with copy of {\ttfamily val} value and then inserts the node created into the set.

The type {\ttfamily Q} should contain as minimum the complete key for the node. The object of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}} should be constructible from a value of type {\ttfamily Q}. In trivial case, {\ttfamily Q} is equal to {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\+\_\+type}}.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_a7fd62d43b7587b8a61003518ccccac74}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!list\_statistics@{list\_statistics}}

Updates the node 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If {\ttfamily key} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily key} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found.

The functor {\ttfamily func} signature depends of ordered list\+:

{\bfseries{for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_michael_list}{Michael\+List}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_lazy_list}{Lazy\+List}}}} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{Q}}\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}.

{\bfseries{for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}}}} 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{val}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a70ee3f6a13d5a1aa7b59cf26977fa4a3}{value\_type}}\ *\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{old}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ a new data constructed from {\ttfamily key} 
\item {\ttfamily old} -\/ old value that will be retired. If new item has been inserted then {\ttfamily old} is {\ttfamily nullptr}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is true if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is true if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the set.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_hp}{Michael\+List} and \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list_cds_nonintrusive_IterableList_gc}{Iterable\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_cds_intrusive_LazyList_hp}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8266c3b915a3db96441e4ec78d3fd377}\index{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$@{cds::container::SplitListSet$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, T, Traits $>$}!update@{update}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{update()}{update()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a8266c3b915a3db96441e4ec78d3fd377} 
template$<$class RCU, class \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{cds\+::container\+::\+Split\+List\+Set}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates an element with given {\ttfamily val} 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the {\ttfamily val} key not found in the set, then the new item created from {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with the item found. The functor {\ttfamily Func} signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{my\_functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{operator()}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{item}},\ \textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_split_list_set}{val}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily ensure}() function
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is true if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is true if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the set. Updates the node The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If {\ttfamily key} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily key} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found.

The functor signature is\+:

with arguments\+:

\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor may change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

Returns {\ttfamily  std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ } where {\ttfamily first} is true if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is true if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already is in the map.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
For \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_michael_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_MichaelList_rcu}{Michael\+List} as the bucket see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting}. \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_lazy_list_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_LazyList_rcu}{Lazy\+List} provides exclusive access to inserted item and does not require any node-\/level synchronization.

Inserts or updates the node (only for {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1container_1_1_iterable_list}{Iterable\+List}} -\/based set) 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the current element is changed to {\ttfamily val}, the old element will be retired later.

Returns std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with that key already in the set.
